## Definitions

  <a id="1755" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="1756" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#1756" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="1759" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#1759" class="Bound">l2</a> <a ### The gap-map into the canonical pullback

The gap map of a square is the map fron the vertex of the cone into the
canonical pullback.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="2173" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="2180" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#2180" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="2184" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2185" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#2185" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="2188" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#2188" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="2191" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#2191" class="Bound">l3</a> <a id="2194" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#2194" class="Bound">l4</a> <a id="2197" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2199" href="Agda.Primitive.html#591" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="2204" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="2206" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2207" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#2207" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="2209" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2211" href="Agda.Primitive.html#320" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="2214" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#2185" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="2216" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="2218" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2219" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#2219" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="2221" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2223" href="Agda.Primitive.html#320" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="2226" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#2188" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="2228" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="2230" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2231" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#2231" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="2233" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2235" href="Agda.Primitive.html#320" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="2238" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#2191" class="Bound">l3</a><a id="2240" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="2242" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2243" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#2243" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="2245" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2247" href="Agda.Primitive.html#320" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="2250" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#2194" class="Bound">l4</a><a id="2252" class="Symbol">}</a>

### The `is-pullback` property

The proposition `is-pullback` is the assertion that the gap map is an
equivalence. Note that this proposition is small, whereas the universal property
is a large proposition.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="2708" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="2715" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#2715" class="Module">_</a>

### The canonical pullback satisfies the universal property of pullbacks

<pre class="Agda"><a id="5730" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="5737" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#5737" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="5741" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5742" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#5742" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="5745" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#5745" class="Bound">l2</a> <a   <a id="5822" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="5831" class="Keyword">abstract</a>

### The pullback of a Σ-type

<pre class="Agda"><a id="8014" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="8021" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#8021" class="Module">_</a>

### Pullbacks are symmetric

<pre class="Agda"><a id="map-commutative-canonical-pullback"></a><a id="9783" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#9783" class="Function">map-commutative-canonical-pullback</a> <a id="9818" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="9822" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9823" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#9823" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="9826" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#9826" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="9829" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#9829" class="Bound">l3</a> <a id="9832" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9834" href="Agda.Primitive.html#591" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="9839" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9841" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9842" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#9842" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9844" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9846" href="Agda.Primitive.html#320" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="9849" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#9823" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="9851" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9853" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9854" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#9854" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="9856" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9858" href="Agda.Primitive.html#320" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="9861" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#9826" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="9863" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9865" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9866" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#9866" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="9868" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9870" href="Agda.Primitive.html#320" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="9873" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#9829" class="Bound">l3</a><a id="9875" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="9879" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9880" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#9880" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="9882" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9884" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#9842" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9886" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9888" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#9866" class="Bound">X</a><a id="9889" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9891" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9892" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#9892" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="9894" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9896" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#9854" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="9898" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9900" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#9866" class="Bound">X</a><a id="9901" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9903" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9905" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#1343" class="Function">canonical-pullback</a> <a id="9924" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#9880" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="9926" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#9892" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="9928" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9930" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#1343" class="Function">canonical-pullback</a> <a id="9949" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#9892" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="9951" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#9880" class="Bound">f</a>

### A family of maps over a base map induces a pullback square if and only if it is a family of equivalences

### A cone is a pullback if and only if it induces a family of equivalences between the fibers of the vertical maps

<pre class="Agda"><a id="24581" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="24588" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#24588" class="Module">_</a>
